  <span id="freeText3666246854301123450" style="display:none">As always with this author, I loved the book. Colleen Hoover has a magical way of yanking you into a story that once I start, I won't stop until I'm finished. It's like living inside the story while I'm reading it. Once again, another 5 star review for one of my favourite authors ! <br /><br />I know I'm not the best reviewer, not even close. I seemed to have lost my way when it comes to writing anything, something I was really good at once upon a time not that long ago. <br />Before I retired, the job I had consisted of coming up with facts and figures that would allow me to put a story together to rationalize a decision that had to be made and I was pretty good at doing that. <br /><br />In the last few years, my health hasn't been good which accounts in part for some of the loss of my vocabulary skills.<br /><br />Not that this will be read because it seems my reviews don't get read, and that's ok. I'm not feeling sorry for myself yet I wonder why I continue to write any review at all since I rarely get a "like" or comment. <br /><br />I understand there are alot of amazing reviewers on GR and I'm grateful for them. They've helped me choose new authors, make decisions on which book I'd rather buy and I truly appreciate how well written many of the reviews are. <br /><br />So I think that I will refrain from writing reviews (unless it's for my own purposes for future reads) and spend more time just reading other reviews. <br /><br />Its something I really enjoy and it gives me the opportunity to find some great books. <br /><br />Thanks to all the great reviewers who have a phenomenal way with words, honestly its a big help and also interesting to read another person's perspective.</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer8855886039883891924"> <i>An epic girlneeds an equally epic guy, and I guess I’ve never felt epic enough for you.</i>*Swoon*<br/><br/> The hype is real! This book was so Flippin’ fantastic! All the feels, not one but two epic love stories, a real and raw look at the mother daughter relationship, tragedy, grief, forgiveness, romance, love, acceptance.   <span id="freeText8855886039883891924" style="display:none"> <i>An epic girlneeds an equally epic guy, and I guess I’ve never felt epic enough for you.</i>*Swoon*<br /><br /> The hype is real! This book was so Flippin’ fantastic! All the feels, not one but two epic love stories, a real and raw look at the mother daughter relationship, tragedy, grief, forgiveness, romance, love, acceptance. Colleen Hoover is an absolute rockstar and this is one of her very best!<br /><br /> Hoover’s exceptional storytelling completely Drew me into these characters lives. The story is told from the alternating perspectives of mother Morgan and daughter Clara. I was equally invested in both characters, I cried with them, I laughed with them, I loved with them, I got angry with them, and I forgave with them. Not only does CoHo tell and engaging tale, she also writes some of the most swoon worthy men/boys. Jonah and Miller *swoon* I think technically I could probably be the mother of both of these men, but wow they really knew how to treat a girl and be there for her. Definitely not a book to be missed! If you are a CoHo fan this will more than likely be one of your favorites, and if you have not read her yet.... What are you waiting for?<br /><br />This book in emojis 👩‍👧 🎭 🎬 🎥 💔 💞<br /><br />*** Big thank you to Amazon Pub for my gifted copy of this book. All opinions are my own. *** <br /><br />For more of my reviews and bookish thoughts please visit <a> my blog </a> <br /><br />🏆 one of my top reads of 2019! <br /><br />🎉🎉🎉 UPDATE this book is available in print and audio on KU!<br /><br />Now I have an audio copy, a print copy, and a digital copy, the question is what am I waiting for? I want to cherish this book so I’m waiting for the perfect time and I’m thinking it is this week!<br /><br />This book is now downloaded onto my Kindle and I could not be more excited!!!💕💕</span>

<div id="review_2944713582" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2944713582" />
    <a title="Jonetta" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4876540-jonetta"><img alt="Jonetta" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1329083158p2/4876540.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2944713582?book_show_action=true">Apr 27, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jonetta" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jonetta" href="/user/show/4876540-jonetta">Jonetta</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Audio CD 9781799723066" href="/book/show/49624390-regretting-you">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4876540-jonetta?shelf=2020-in-2020">2020-in-2020</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4876540-jonetta?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4876540-jonetta?shelf=audiobook">audiobook</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4876540-jonetta?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4876540-jonetta?shelf=5000-2020">5000-2020</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4876540-jonetta?shelf=2020-beat-the-backlist-challenge">2020-beat-the-backlist-challenge</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4876540-jonetta?shelf=publisher-review-request">publisher-review-request</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4876540-jonetta?shelf=2020-audiobook-challenge">2020-audiobook-challenge</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2944713582" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16724559382502441182">Morgan Grant is married and the mother of soon-to-be 17-year old daughter, Clara. One day after her own birthday, Morgan is suddenly thrust into chaos when her world is forever changed following a tragic accident involving her husband, Chris. While her relationship with her daughter was not bad, it wasn’t great and he was the one who helped mediate the rocky moments. Further complicating matters is Clara’s budding relationship with a boy Chris wasn’t happy about her getting involved with. Morgan</span>
  <span id="freeText16724559382502441182" style="display:none">Morgan Grant is married and the mother of soon-to-be 17-year old daughter, Clara. One day after her own birthday, Morgan is suddenly thrust into chaos when her world is forever changed following a tragic accident involving her husband, Chris. While her relationship with her daughter was not bad, it wasn’t great and he was the one who helped mediate the rocky moments. Further complicating matters is Clara’s budding relationship with a boy Chris wasn’t happy about her getting involved with. Morgan has her own angst to manage while struggling to maintain some parental control over her daughter without sacrificing the bond that’s barely holding them together. <br /><br />I’ve often seen the phrase, “all the feels” used in describing emotional stories and particularly those by this author. It never really resonated with me...until this one. I’ll not give you many details as they would definitely ruin your personal reading experience so here’s what mattered to me. <br /><br />Morgan got handed situations she neither deserved or felt prepared for. Imagine dealing with grief, new responsibilities, emotional trauma coming from new situations while trying to find work after never having had a job and dealing with a teenager who wants to direct all that’s wrong in her world at you. I felt every pain, fear, anxiety and consternation that Morgan did. My emotions were all over the place, wondering how she was going to navigate the next ball being thrown at her. Would it be a direct hit or something she could drop without too much consequence? Handling it wasn’t always a good option. <br /><br />I literally could not stop listening to this book. When I took a break to sleep, I woke at a ridiculous hour the next morning so I could get back to it. It’s a tale of two points of view as you get Clara’s, too. Because it’s from a teenager’s perspective, it has both young adult and contemporary adult fiction components and I’ve shelved this in both genres. I loved that two narrators were used and both did a fantastic job portraying Morgan and Clara, almost too good as they grabbed me by the throat from the start and tore up my insides. Obviously I loved everything about this one but don’t go into this thinking it will be all sweetness and light. It’s there but you’ve got to pay a steep price for it. And I wouldn’t have it any other way. <br /><br /><i>Posted on</i> <a href="https://wp.me/p49DcV-1nC" rel="nofollow noopener">Blue Mood Café</a><br /><br />(Thanks to Brilliance Audio for my complimentary copy. All opinions are my own.)</span>
  <a data-text-id="16724559382502441182" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2768385312?book_show_action=true">Mar 29, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Amy | Foxy Blogs" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Amy | Foxy Blogs" href="/user/show/9955253-amy-foxy-blogs">Amy | Foxy Blogs</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9955253-amy-foxy-blogs?shelf=arc-or-netgalley">arc-or-netgalley</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2768385312" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2714791524064816982"><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1553924231ra/27288434.gif' width='' height='' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>NO REGRETS GIVEN!!</b> This book was something I couldn’t put down. I spent my birthday reading it. I took a break to go to lunch with my husband and then came home and finished it. It was the most amazing birthday gift I gave to myself: spending the day with no distractions and reading <b>Regretting You!</b> <br/> <br/>I’m calling it now: it’s <b>my new favorite CoHo book.</b> Okay, maybe I should say it’s tied with my longtime CoHo favorite,<i> Hopeless.</i> I guess in some ways they have a similar vibe and in other ways, they </span>
  <span id="freeText2714791524064816982" style="display:none"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1553924231ra/27288434.gif" width="" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>NO REGRETS GIVEN!!</b> This book was something I couldn’t put down. I spent my birthday reading it. I took a break to go to lunch with my husband and then came home and finished it. It was the most amazing birthday gift I gave to myself: spending the day with no distractions and reading <b>Regretting You!</b> <br> <br>I’m calling it now: it’s <b>my new favorite CoHo book.</b> Okay, maybe I should say it’s tied with my longtime CoHo favorite,<i> Hopeless.</i> I guess in some ways they have a similar vibe and in other ways, they are totally different. <br><br><b>
  <i>“Life doesn’t play favorites.”</i>
</b><br><br>The truth behind that quote is smack dab the essence of this book. You can be a good person and do all the “right” things by being selfless and life can still knock you down and leave you wondering what you ever did to deserve this type of treatment. Regretting You is a story about how messy life can be and how family ties bond us together. The story alternates between a mother, Morgan, and her teenage daughter, Carla. Readers view the world through their eyes. <br><br>The story is immersed in a tragic event that pulls on everyone’s heartstrings, even the readers. When secrets are brought to the forefront, everyone's world becomes a lot messier. <br><br>There were times in the book where I wore a shocked look on my face and other times when my heart broke. At times I laughed and other times I swooned. <b> It’s a story full of FEELS.</b><br><br>✦✦✦✦✦✦✦✦✦✦✦✦✦✦✦✦✦✦✦✦✦✦✦✦✦✦✦<br>RELEASE DATE: December 10, 2019<br>Pre-order | order: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://amzn.to/2IKYTl0">https://amzn.to/2IKYTl0</a><br><br>**Complimentary copy in exchange for an honest review.**<br><a href="http://foxyblogs.com" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1442610494i/16258382._SX540_.jpg" width="400" alt="descriptive text here" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('1uqFoqtlujFE62ghsmv+1EVIUTGlhnAnZLrBKMQ2dIzcIX9fmOmgIbGNM3VKuWi+vYKkMZlEz9lISnl6eLbv4A==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('ewDUYlEm18CwQIPiJ+LoGN285ImIvinGFE6H4E/ESc5xyy6fYqrN0EUm2LbfMH5yJXYRibR8ljg4vj+y80TSog==')})
  }
//]]>

      <div class=" clearFloats bigBox"><div class="h2Container gradientHeaderContainer"><h2 class="brownBackground"><a href="/work/quotes/69199213-regretting-you">Quotes from Regretting You</a></h2></div><div class="bigBoxBody"><div class="bigBoxContent containerWithHeaderContent">
          <div class="stacked" tyle="padding-bottom:15px">
            <span class="readable">&ldquo;Attraction isn’t something that only happens once, with one person. It’s part of what drives humans. Our attraction to each other, to art, to food, to entertainment. Attraction is fun. So when you decide to commit to someone, you aren’t saying, ‘I promise I’ll never be attracted to anyone else.’ You’re saying, ‘I promise to commit to you, despite my potential future attraction to other people.’” I look at Clara. “Relationships are hard for that very reason. Your body and your heart don’t stop finding the beauty and the attraction in other people simply because you’ve made a commitment to one person. If you ever find yourself in a situation where you’re drawn to someone else, it’s up to you to remove yourself from that situation before it becomes too hard to fight.&rdquo;</span>
            <nobr>
              &mdash;
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/quotes/10087762-attraction-isn-t-something-that-only-happens-once-with-one-person">75 likes</a>

        script.type = 'text/javascript';
        script.async = true;
        script.src = load[i];
        first.parentNode.insertBefore(script, first);
      }
    }
  if (w.attachEvent) {
    w.attachEvent('onload', go);
  } else {
    w.addEventListener('load', go, false);
  }
}(window, document,
    ['//assets.pinterest.com/js/pinit.js',
     '//apis.google.com/js/plusone.js'
    ]
  ));

//]]>
</script>
